#exp_behavior

behavior find_cup_2087_around_kitchen_counter_132(cup:item):
    goal: not unknown(cup)
    body:
        assert is_cup(cup)
        bind kitchen_counter_instance:item where:
            is_kitchen_counter(kitchen_counter_instance) and id[kitchen_counter_instance]==132
        achieve close_char(char,kitchen_counter_instance)
        if can_open(kitchen_counter_instance):
            achieve_once open(kitchen_counter_instance)
            exp(cup,kitchen_counter_instance)
        else:
            exp(cup,kitchen_counter_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[cup]=False
        close[cup,kitchen_counter_instance]=True
        close[kitchen_counter_instance,cup]=True
    

behavior find_milk_2074_around_fridge_140(milk:item):
    goal: not unknown(milk)
    body:
        assert is_milk(milk)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==140
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)
            exp(milk,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(milk,fridge_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[milk]=False
        close[milk,fridge_instance]=True
        close[fridge_instance,milk]=True
    

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation

def has_cup_or_milk_in_kitchen():
    # Function to check if there are cups or milk in the kitchen
    symbol has_cup_or_milk=exists o: item : ((is_cup(o) or is_milk(o)) and inside(o, kitchen))
    return has_cup_or_milk

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        if exists kitchen: item : is_kitchen(kitchen) and has_cup_or_milk_in_kitchen():
            # If we have already found the kitchen with cups or milk, we can directly approach it
            bind kitchen: item where:
                is_kitchen(kitchen) and has_cup_or_milk_in_kitchen()
            walk_to(kitchen)

        else:
            # Check all unvisited rooms in the scene to find the kitchen
            foreach room: item:
                if is_kitchen(room) and not visited(room):
                    observe(room,"Check is there any cup or milk in the kitchen")

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior find_cup():
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if is_cup(item) and not visited(item):
                observe(item, "Check if it is a cup")

behavior find_milk():
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if is_milk(item) and not visited(item):
                observe(item, "Check if it is milk")

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        find_cup()
        find_milk()


#goal_representation_end

#exp_behavior

behavior find_cup_2087_around_kitchen_counter_132(cup:item):
    goal: not unknown(cup)
    body:
        assert is_cup(cup)
        bind kitchen_counter_instance:item where:
            is_kitchen_counter(kitchen_counter_instance) and id[kitchen_counter_instance]==132
        achieve close_char(char,kitchen_counter_instance)
        if can_open(kitchen_counter_instance):
            achieve_once open(kitchen_counter_instance)
            exp(cup,kitchen_counter_instance)
        else:
            exp(cup,kitchen_counter_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[cup]=False
        close[cup,kitchen_counter_instance]=True

def is_cup_grabbed():
    # Check if a cup has been grabbed
    symbol grabbed=exists o: item : (is_cup(o) and inhand(o))
    return grabbed

def is_milk_grabbed():
    # Check if milk has been grabbed
    symbol grabbed=exists o: item : (is_milk(o) and inhand(o))
    return grabbed

def has_milk_inside(cup:item):
    # Check if the cup has milk inside
    symbol has_milk=exists o: item : (is_milk(o) and inside(o, cup))
    return has_milk

behavior grab_cup():
    body:
        bind cup: item where:
            is_cup(cup) and grabbable(cup) and not inhand(cup) and not visited(cup)
        if not is_cup_grabbed():
            grab(cup)

behavior pour_milk(cup:item):
    body:
        bind milk: item where:
            is_milk(milk) and grabbable(milk) and not inhand(milk) and not visited(milk)
        if has_a_free_hand(char) and not is_milk_grabbed():
            grab(milk)
        if is_milk_grabbed() and recipient(cup) and not has_milk_inside(cup):
            put_inside(milk, cup)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        grab_cup()
        bind cup: item where:
            is_cup(cup) and inhand(cup)
        pour_milk(cup)

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior heat_milk_in_microwave(cup_of_milk: item, microwave: item):
    body:
        if not inside(cup_of_milk, microwave):
            put_inside(cup_of_milk, microwave)
        if open(microwave):
            closes(microwave) # Close the microwave
        if is_off(microwave):
            switch_on(microwave) # Turn on the microwave to heat the milk

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind cup_of_milk: item where:
            is_cup(cup_of_milk) and inhand(cup_of_milk)
        # The cup with milk is already in hand
        bind microwave: item where:
            is_microwave(microwave)
        heat_milk_in_microwave(cup_of_milk, microwave)

#goal_representation_end
